<div id="overview-content" class="sku-number">
	<article class="a_plus_content">
		
		<div><img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/logo.png" alt="Logo" class="logovc"></div>	
		
		<div class="a_plus_module content_float">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/p0.jpg" alt="img" class="img_f_left">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info txt_f_right">
        <h3 class="title_1"><strong>HUAWEI</strong> WiFi AX3 </h3>
				<h3 class="title_2">Quad-core Wi-Fi 6 Plus Revolution</h3>
				
      	<p>Arm your home network with next-generation Wi-Fi 6 with HUAWEI WiFi AX3 wireless router. It brings all the benefits of Wi-Fi 6 technology, including super-fast speeds, high capacity, low latency, and more. When paired with Wi-Fi 6 enabled HUAWEI phones, it will give you even faster speeds of up to 3000 Mbps,<sup>1</sup> stronger signals, and more stable connections. </p>
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="section_head">Usher in the Era of Wi-Fi 6 </div><br>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module space_0">
      <div class="a_plus_info">
      	<p class="center">Wi-Fi 5 is the standard used by most devices today, while Wi-Fi 6 (802.11ax) is the new standard that's gradually coming into smart devices in recent years. Wi-Fi 6 has made several improvements over Wi-Fi 5 to cope with the increasing demand for faster and more efficient Wi-Fi. </p>
      </div>
	  </div> 
		
		<div class="four_columns">
      <div class="a_plus_column">
      	<img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/1a.png" alt="img">

      	<div class="a_plus_info">
          <h3 class="title_2">3 X Faster Speed </h3>	
          <p>With 1024-QAM and 160 MHz bandwidth, the overall speed of Wi-Fi 6 is greatly boosted.<sup>2</sup> </p>
      	</div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="a_plus_column">
      	<img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/1b.png" alt="img">

      	<div class="a_plus_info">
          <h3 class="title_2">4 X Larger Capacity </h3>	
          <p>Wi-Fi 6 (with OFDMA) allows the router to connect more devices simultaneously with little slowdown.<sup>2</sup> </p>
      	</div>
      </div>
			
			<div class="a_plus_column">
      	<img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/1c.png" alt="img">

      	<div class="a_plus_info">
          <h3 class="title_2">2/3 Lowered Latency </h3>	
          <p>Wi-Fi 6 allows you to enjoy faster response when connecting to multiple devices.<sup>2</sup> </p>
      	</div>
      </div>
			
			<div class="a_plus_column">
      	<img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/1d.png" alt="img">

      	<div class="a_plus_info">
          <h3 class="title_2">30% Reduced Power Consumption </h3>	
          <p>Negotiate wake-up time among connected devices to avoid consuming power while waiting/on standby.<sup>2</sup> </p>
      	</div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="clearvc"></div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="section_head">Take a Step Further with HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6 Plus</div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/2.jpg" alt="img"> 
         
      <div class="a_plus_info right_b">
      	<h3 class="title_1">Speed up—HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6-Enabled Phones with HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6 Plus </h3>
      	
      	<p class="color_b">AX3 and Wi-Fi 6-enabled HUAWEI phones are the perfect pair because both are equipped with HUAWEI's self-developed Wi-Fi chipset, which supports 160 MHz frequency bandwidth. This lays the foundation for Chipset Synergy, bringing out optimal speed and efficiency. </p>
      </div>
    </div>
		
		 <div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/3.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_b">
        <h3 class="title_1 center">Signal Can Go Through One More Wall with HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6 Plus<sup>3</sup> </h3>
   
        <p class="color_b center">HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6-enabled phones are able to send 6dB stronger signals back to AX3 in stable, 2 MHz narrow bandwidth using Dynamic Narrow Bandwidth technology, which is based on Chipset Synergy. The wireless signals can penetrate solid objects like walls and floors easily. This means that the phone will have good reception of the Wi-Fi signal even when connecting from upstairs or somewhere far from the router. </p>  
      </div>
    </div>
		
		 <div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/4.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_b">
        <h3 class="title_1 center">Fast Speed beyond Your Imagination </h3>
   
        <p class="color_b center">You will be impressed with the blazing fast speed delivered by AX3. Thanks to 1024-QAM and 160 MHz frequency bandwidth, its theoretical speed can reach up to 3000 Mbps (574 Mbps on a 2.4 GHz band and 2402 Mbps on a 5 GHz band).<sup>1</sup> The quad-core Gigahome CPU allows AX3 to best unleash its speed. At such speed, what used to be taken for granted, like buffering and lagging, will be a thing of the past. Enjoy smooth streaming and gaming like never before. </p>  
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/5.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_w">
      	<h3 class="title_1 color_w center">Multiple Connections. Smooth Connections. </h3>
      	
      	<p class="color_w2 center">Unlike traditional routers, you can connect a multitude of devices to AX3 with greater efficiency. Supporting OFDMA multi-user technology, it is capable to send data to multiple devices simultaneously (max. 4 devices on 2.4 GHz, max. 16 devices on 5 GHz). The highly powered quad-core Gigahome CPU also ensures smooth running of the processor. And, it is capable of connecting up to 128 devices overall on dual bands.<sup>4</sup> No matter how crowded the space, it will serve different users and devices promptly. </p>
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/6.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_b">
        <h3 class="title_1 center">Larger Bandwidth with 160 MHz </h3>
   
        <p class="color_b center">As AX3 supports 160 MHz, when connecting AX3 to devices supporting 160 MHz, like top-of-the-line HUAWEI Wi-Fi 5-enabled smart phones, tablets and laptops, the internet speed would increase 60% and more.<sup>5</sup> This offers you an unprecedented, lag-free experience on mobile devices. </p>  
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/7.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_b">
      	<h3 class="title_1 color_b center">Effortless Connection, Revolutionary Experience </h3>
      	
      	<p class="color_b center">Huawei Share<sup>6</sup> allows you to connect AX3 to your smart phone with a simple tap. Whether throwing a home party or celebrating festivals with friends and families, this router will remember the password for you and let the guests you trust, connect to it easily. </p>
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/8.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_b">
        <h3 class="title_1 center">Multi-router mesh networking<sup>7</sup> enables greater Wi-Fi coverage </h3>
   
        <p class="color_b center">The HUAWEI WiFi AX3 supports wireless networking, network cable networking, and the hybrid networking of wireless and network cables. After networking, multiple routers are automatically grouped under one Wi-Fi name, and the optimal Wi-Fi is automatically selected based on the device's location. The HUAWEI WiFi AX3 can network with old HUAWEI Wi-Fi routers (with H button) to expand network coverage at home. </p>  
      </div>
    </div>
		
		<div class="a_plus_module text_on_img space_0">
      <img src="//images10.newegg.com/BizIntell/item/Network Retail/Network - Wireless Routers/33-624-001/9.jpg" alt="img">
      
      <div class="a_plus_info center_w">
      	<h3 class="title_1 color_w center">Protect Your Network with Huawei HomeSec </h3>
      	
      	<p class="color_w2 center">Enabled by TEE (Trusted Execution Environment) and Microkernel, AX3 offers a secure area inside its main processor, where both software and hardware are used to protect the data. It is also CC EAL5 certified, meaning it could operate safely in a commercial environment, offering great security assurance to your devices. </p>
      </div>
    </div><br>
		
		 <div class="a_plus_module space_0">
      <div class="a_plus_info" style="padding:0 3%;">				
        <h3 class="title_1 ov_note">
        Note:
        </h3>
        	
        <p class="ov_note">1.This is the theoretical maximum speed of HUAWEI WiFi AX3. Actual speed may vary depending on the environment and devices. </p>
				<p class="ov_note">2.Data from HUAWEI lab, by comparing Wi-Fi 5 and Wi-Fi 6 technology. Actual results may vary. </p>
        <p class="ov_note">3.Data from HUAWEI lab, by comparing HUAWEI WiFi AX3 with other Wi-Fi 6 router. The signal sent back to AX3 is 6dB stronger, which allows it to pass through one more wall. </p>
				<p class="ov_note">4.Data from HUAWEI lab. Actual results may vary. </p>
        <p class="ov_note">5.Data from HUAWEI lab, using HUAWEI Mate 30 Pro to test the internet speed. </p>	
				<p class="ov_note">6.Supported by NFC-enabled Android phones. Certain Android phones with non-standard NFC may not support Huawei Share. AX3 quad-core version supports Huawei Share, yet the dual-core version does not support. </p>
				<p class="ov_note">7.Huawei routers should have an H button. </p>
      </div>
    </div>

class=\"title_2\"\u003EQuad-core Wi-Fi 6 Plus Revolution\u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n\t\t\t\t\n      \t\u003Cp\u003EArm your home network with next-generation Wi-Fi 6 with HUAWEI WiFi AX3 wireless router. It brings all the benefits of Wi-Fi 6 technology, including super-fast speeds, high capacity, low latency, and more. When paired with Wi-Fi 6 enabled HUAWEI phones, it will give you even faster speeds of up to 3000 Mbps,\u003Csup\u003E1\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E stronger signals, and more stable connections. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n      \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n    \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n\t\t\n\t\t\u003Cdiv class=\"section_head\"\u003EUsher in the Era of Wi-Fi 6 \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cbr\u003E\n\t\t\n\t\t\u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_module space_0\"\u003E\n      \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_info\"\u003E\n      \t\u003Cp class=\"center\"\u003EWi-Fi 5 is the standard used by most devices today, while Wi-Fi 6 (802.11ax) is the new standard that's gradually coming into smart devices in recent years. Wi-Fi 6 has made several improvements over Wi-Fi 5 to cope with the increasing demand for faster and more efficient Wi-Fi. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n      \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n\t  \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E \n\t\t\n\t\t\u003Cdiv class=\"four_columns\"\u003E\n      \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_column\"\u003E\n      \t\u003Cimg src=\"\u002F\u002Fimages10.newegg.com\u002FBizIntell\u002Fitem\u002FNetwork Retail\u002FNetwork - This lays the foundation for Chipset Synergy, bringing out optimal speed and efficiency. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n      \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n    \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n\t\t\n\t\t \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_module text_on_img space_0\"\u003E\n      \u003Cimg src=\"\u002F\u002Fimages10.newegg.com\u002FBizIntell\u002Fitem\u002FNetwork Retail\u002FNetwork - Wireless Routers\u002F33-624-001\u002F3.jpg\" alt=\"img\"\u003E\n      \n      \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_info center_b\"\u003E\n        \u003Ch3 class=\"title_1 center\"\u003ESignal Can Go Through One More Wall with HUAWEI Wi-Fi 6 Plus\u003Csup\u003E3\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E \u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n   \n        \u003Cp class=\"color_b center\"\u003EHUAWEI Wi-Fi 6-enabled phones are able to send 6dB stronger signals back to AX3 in stable, 2 MHz narrow bandwidth using Dynamic Narrow Bandwidth technology, which is based on Chipset Synergy. The wireless signals can penetrate solid objects like walls and floors easily. This means that the phone will have good reception of the Wi-Fi signal even when connecting from upstairs or somewhere far from the router. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E  \n      \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n    \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n\t\t\n\t\t \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_module text_on_img space_0\"\u003E\n      \u003Cimg src=\"\u002F\u002Fimages10.newegg.com\u002FBizIntell\u002Fitem\u002FNetwork Retail\u002FNetwork - Wireless Routers\u002F33-624-001\u002F4.jpg\" alt=\"img\"\u003E\n      \n      \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_info center_b\"\u003E\n        \u003Ch3 class=\"title_1 center\"\u003EFast Speed beyond Your Imagination \u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n   \n        \u003Cp class=\"color_b center\"\u003EYou will be impressed with the blazing fast speed delivered by AX3. Thanks to 1024-QAM and 160 MHz frequency bandwidth, its theoretical speed can reach up to 3000 Mbps (574 Mbps on a 2.4 GHz band and 2402 Mbps on a 5 GHz band).\u003Csup\u003E1\u003C\u002Fsup\u003E The quad-core Gigahome CPU allows AX3 to best unleash its speed. At such speed, what used to be taken for granted, like buffering and lagging, will be a thing of the past. Enjoy smooth streaming and gaming like never before. \u003C\u002Fp\u003E  \n      \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n    \u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\n\t\t\n\t\t\u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_module text_on_img space_0\"\u003E\n      \u003Cimg src=\"\u002F\u002Fimages10.newegg.com\u002FBizIntell\u002Fitem\u002FNetwork Retail\u002FNetwork - Wireless Routers\u002F33-624-001\u002F5.jpg\" alt=\"img\"\u003E\n      \n      \u003Cdiv class=\"a_plus_info center_w\"\u003E\n      \t\u003Ch3 class=\"title_1 color_w center\"\u003EMultiple Connections. Smooth Connections. \u003C\u002Fh3\u003E\n      \t\n      \t\u003Cp class=\"color_w2 center\"\u003EUnlike traditional routers, you can connect a multitude of devices to AX3 with greater efficiency.
